### <a id="the-inductive-types-h-s-p-v">The Inductive Types H, S, P, V</a>

This section presents the [Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="329" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="333" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="341" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="367" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="374" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="379" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="391" href="Algebras.Signatures.html" class="Module">Algebras.Signatures</a> <a id="411" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="418" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="427" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="429" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5600" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="430" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="432" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="433" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="435" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="440" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="447" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="473" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="480" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="494" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="497" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="504" href="Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="524" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="527" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="529" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="539" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5600" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="541" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="542" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="544" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="550" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="564" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="566" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="573" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="578" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="585" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">Varieties.EquationalLogic</a><a id="610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="611" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="613" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="616" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="623" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="630" class="Comment">--open import MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems using (hfunext) -- public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3624" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3629" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3631" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3632" <a id="4124" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4125" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4127" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4129" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4131" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4133" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4134" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4135" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4136" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4138" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4139" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4141" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4143" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4145" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4093" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4147" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4149" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4110" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4151" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4153" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4110" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4155" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4157" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4159" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4162" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4169" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4171" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4172" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4174" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4176" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4178" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4186" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4188" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4189" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4191" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4193" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4195" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4198" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4199" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4200" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4202" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3634" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4203" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4207" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4209" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4172" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4211" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4213" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4215" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4217" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4174" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4219" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4221" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4223" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3648" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4563" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4568" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4570" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4571" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4573" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4577" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="4585" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4591" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="4595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4596" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4606" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4607" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4633" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4635" id="5216" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5217" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5220" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5222" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5224" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5226" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5173" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5228" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5230" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5232" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5235" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5235" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5244" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5245" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5249" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5257" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5259" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5260" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5262" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5266" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5274" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5276" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5277" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5279" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5281" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5283" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5287" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5288" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5290" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5291" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5295" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5245" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5299" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5303" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5305" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5262" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5307" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5309" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5311" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5314" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5321" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5324" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5326" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5330" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5338" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5341" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5343" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5345" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5347" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5351" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4571" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5352" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5354" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4573" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5355" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5357" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5359" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5361" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5324" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5363" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5365" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5367" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5369" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5326" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5371" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5373" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5375" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4587" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5738" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5740" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5741" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5743" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5745" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5753" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5755" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5757" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5759" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5765" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5773" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5776" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5778" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5782" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5785" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5787" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5741" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5792" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5794" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5804" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5806" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5808" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5810" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5812" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5813" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5815" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5817" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5805" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5818" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5822" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5808" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5827" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5827" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5835" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5837" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5838" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5838" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5842" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5850" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5852" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5854" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5855" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5858" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5838" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5859" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5860" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5862" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5864" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5827" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5874" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5876" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5878" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5878" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5880" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5883" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5889" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5897" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5899" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5900" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5902" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5905" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5872" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5906" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5909" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5911" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5727" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5922" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5878" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6391" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6396" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2741" class="Module">Lift</a>
<a id="6401" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6408" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6408" class="Module">_</a> <a id="6410" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6411" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6413" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6415" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="6423" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6427" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6429" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6434" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6435" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6443" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6445" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6446" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6448" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6451" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6452" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6455" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="6463" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6470" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6474" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6483" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6487" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6489" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6490" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="6494" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6499" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6501" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6503" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6504" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6505" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6506" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6508" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6511" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6512" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6514" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
       <a id="6523" class="Comment">--------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="6564" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6569" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6578" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6470" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6581" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6584" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6586" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6587" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6589" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6591" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6592" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6593" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6594" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6596" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6599" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6411" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6601" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6602" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6425" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="6608" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6613" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4659" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a><a id="6618" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6619" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6619" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6620" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6622" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6623" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6625" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6627" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="6633" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6634" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4659" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a> <a id="6640" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6622" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6641" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6643" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6644" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6412" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="6665" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6619" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6666" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="6669" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6674" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4716" class="InductiveConstructor">vlift</a><a id="6679" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6680" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6680" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6681" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6683" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6683" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6684" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6686" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6688" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="6694" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6695" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4716" class="InductiveConstructor">vlift</a> <a id="6701" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6683" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6702" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6705" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6412" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="6726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6680" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6727" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="7763" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7763" class="Function">iso-components</a> <a id="7778" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7780" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7781" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7783" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7785" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7463" class="Bound">I</a><a id="7786" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7788" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7790" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7466" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="7792" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7781" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7794" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="7796" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7620" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="7799" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7800" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2803" class="InductiveConstructor">lift</a> <a id="7805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7781" class="Bound">i</a><a id="7806" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="7810" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7763" class="Function">iso-components</a> <a id="7825" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7825" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7827" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7829" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4857" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a>

  <a id="7843" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7843" class="Function">B≅A</a> <a id="7847" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7849" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7560" class="Function">lA+</a> <a id="7853" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="7855" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="7857" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7620" class="Function">lA</a>
  <a id="7862" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7843" class="Function">B≅A</a> <a id="7866" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7868" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7896" class="Function">lift-alg-⨅≅</a> <a id="7880" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="7884" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7763" class="Function">iso-components</a>

 <a id="7901" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7905" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7906" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5235" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a><a id="7911" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7912" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7912" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7913" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7915" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7915" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7916" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7918" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7918" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7920" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7920" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7923" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7925" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7927" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7933" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7934" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4716" class="InductiveConstructor">vlift</a> <a id="7940" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7918" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7941" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7943" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7944" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5707" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="7957" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7920" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7960" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="7963" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7968" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a><a id="7973" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7974" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7974" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7975" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7977" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7977" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7978" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7980" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7980" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7982" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7982" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7985" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7987" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7989" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7995" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7996" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="8000" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7980" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8001" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8003" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8004" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5707" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="8017" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7982" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="8020" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P-mono"></a><a id="8452" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8452" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="8459" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8462" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8462" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8464" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8464" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8466" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8468" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="8476" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8478" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8478" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8480" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8480" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="8483" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8485" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="8489" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8490" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8498" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8462" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8500" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8501" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8503" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8506" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8462" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8507" class="Symbol">)}</a>

  <a id="9138" class="Symbol">→</a>        <a id="9147" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="9148" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9149" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9071" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9151" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9153" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9073" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9154" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9156" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9071" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9158" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9160" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9073" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9161" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9163" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9164" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="9165" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9166" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9071" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9167" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9169" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9071" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9171" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9173" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9073" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9174" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9176" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9106" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="9177" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9179" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9181" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="9182" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9183" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9071" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9184" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9186" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9071" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9188" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9190" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9073" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9191" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9193" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9106" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="9197" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9095" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9205" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9206" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3720" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="9212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9212" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9213" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9218" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9220" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3842" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftw</a> <a id="9227" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9212" class="Bound">x</a>

 <a id="9316" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9095" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9324" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9325" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3919" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="9331" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9331" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9332" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9337" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9339" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9345" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9348" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9348" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9350" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9352" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9095" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9361" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9331" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9363" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9348" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9364" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="9368" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9095" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9376" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9377" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9383" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9383" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9384" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9389" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9391" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4001" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9397" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9400" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9400" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9402" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9404" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9095" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9412" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9413" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9383" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9415" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9400" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9416" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="9737" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9737" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9744" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9746" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9747" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9749" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9749" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="9751" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9753" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="9761" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9763" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9763" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9765" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9765" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9768" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9770" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9775" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9776" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="9784" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9747" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="9787" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="9789" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9792" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9747" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9793" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="9797" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="9805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9763" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9807" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9809" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9765" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9812" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9815" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9816" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9747" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9817" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9819" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9749" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9820" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9822" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9763" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9824" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9826" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9827" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9828" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9747" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9829" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9831" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9749" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9832" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9834" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9765" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="9838" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9737" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9845" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9845" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9849" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9850" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9856" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9856" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9857" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="9870" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9878" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9879" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9845" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9883" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9856" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9884" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9886" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9737" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9893" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9893" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9898" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="9903" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9904" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9904" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9905" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9907" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9907" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9908" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="9918" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9920" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="9926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9927" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9737" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9934" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9893" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9938" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9907" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9939" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="10326" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10333" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10333" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10335" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10336" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10336" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10338" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10338" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10340" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10342" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="10350" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10352" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10352" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10354" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10356" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10362" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10370" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10336" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10373" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10375" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10378" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10336" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10379" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="10382" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="10390" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10390" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10403" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10405" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10406" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10406" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10410" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10418" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10419" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10336" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10421" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10423" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10338" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10424" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10426" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10427" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10429" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10431" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10406" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10433" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4065" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10453" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10352" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10455" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10457" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10406" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10459" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="10461" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="10462" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10463" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10336" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10464" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10466" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10338" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10467" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10469" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10352" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="10473" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10390" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10486" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10487" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10487" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="10488" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10490" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10491" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10491" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10493" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10495" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10497" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10497" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="10499" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10501" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10501" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="10504" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10506" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10508" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10508" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="10511" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10513" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10513" class="Bound">B≅C</a><a id="10516" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10519" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10521" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="10526" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10642" class="Function">sA</a> <a id="10529" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10544" class="Function">B≤A</a>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="12653" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12435" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="12667" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12668" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12668" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="12669" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="12671" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12671" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="12673" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12676" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12676" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="12678" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12680" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12680" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="12683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12685" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12687" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12687" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="12690" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12692" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12692" class="Bound">B≅C</a> <a id="12696" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12698" class="Symbol">=</a>

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

</pre>



We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

  <a id="15166" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15135" class="Function">h</a> <a id="15168" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15170" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15172" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15172" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15174" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15176" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13573" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="15180" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15182" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15058" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="15187" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15172" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15189" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

  <a id="15219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15194" class="Function">α</a> <a id="15221" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15223" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15225" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15225" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15227" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15227" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15229" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15231" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15232" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15135" class="Function">h</a> <a id="15234" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15227" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15235" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15237" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15238" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15225" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15240" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15227" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15241" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="15440" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15418" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a> <a id="15447" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15449" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15450" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15194" class="Function">α</a> <a id="15452" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15454" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15245" class="Function">β</a><a id="15455" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15457" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15459" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15339" class="Function">γ</a>

  <a id="15464" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15464" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15466" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15468" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="15470" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14898" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="15472" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="15474" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="15476" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14597" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="15480" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15464" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15482" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15484" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3919" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="15490" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15493" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15493" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15495" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15497" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8904" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="15504" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15505" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15507" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13651" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="15511" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15513" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14840" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="15517" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15493" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15519" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15521" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="15522" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="15738" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="15745" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15745" class="Module">_</a> <a id="15747" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15748" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15748" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15752" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="15760" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15762" class="Bound">fe</a> <a id="15765" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15767" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="15775" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15776" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15779" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15748" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15780" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15782" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15785" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15748" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15786" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="15789" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15789" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="15791" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15793" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="15798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15799" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="15807" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15748" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15809" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="15810" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15812" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15815" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15748" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15816" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="15819" class="Keyword">where</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P⊆V"></a><a id="17228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17228" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17232" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17234" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17235" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17235" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17237" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17237" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="17239" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17241" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="17249" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17251" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17251" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17253" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17255" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17260" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17261" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17269" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17235" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17271" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17272" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17274" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17277" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17235" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17278" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17281" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17283" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17284" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17285" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17235" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17286" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17288" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17237" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17289" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17291" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17251" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17293" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17295" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="17296" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17297" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17235" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17298" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17300" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17237" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17301" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17251" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="SP⊆V"></a><a id="17570" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17577" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17578" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17578" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17580" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17580" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="17582" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17584" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="17592" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17594" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17594" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17596" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17598" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17604" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17612" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17578" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17614" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17615" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17617" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17620" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17578" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17621" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="17625" class="Symbol">→</a>     <a id="17631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="17632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17633" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17578" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17635" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17637" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17580" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17638" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17640" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17578" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17642" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17644" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17580" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17645" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17647" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17648" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17649" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17650" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17578" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17651" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17653" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17580" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17654" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17656" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17594" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17657" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17659" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17661" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="17663" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17594" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="17666" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17672" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="17677" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17678" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17678" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17679" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17681" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17681" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="17686" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17688" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17690" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17228" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17694" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17695" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4162" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="17701" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17681" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="17707" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4857" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17717" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17719" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17725" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="17730" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17731" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17731" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17732" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17734" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17734" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17735" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17737" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17739" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4781" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="17746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17752" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17734" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17753" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17755" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17760" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17761" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="17765" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17766" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17766" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17767" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17769" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17769" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17770" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17772" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17772" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17776" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17776" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17779" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17781" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17790" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17796" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17772" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17799" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17801" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17776" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="17805" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17810" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17811" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3229" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="17816" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17817" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17817" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17818" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17820" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17820" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17821" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17823" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17823" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17827" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17827" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17830" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17832" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17834" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17841" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17842" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17847" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17823" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17850" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17852" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17827" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="17856" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17861" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17862" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17867" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17867" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17869" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17869" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="17871" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17873" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17875" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17882" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17887" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17867" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17888" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17890" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17869" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We just proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="18230" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="18237" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18237" class="Module">_</a> <a id="18239" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18240" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18244" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="18252" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18254" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18254" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18256" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18258" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18263" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18264" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18272" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18274" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18275" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18277" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18278" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18281" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18282" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18285" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="18293" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18293" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18299" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18301" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="18302" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18303" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18306" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18307" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18309" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18312" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18314" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18315" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18317" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18318" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="18319" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18320" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18321" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18323" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18326" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18327" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18329" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18254" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18330" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18332" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2729" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="18334" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4568" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="18336" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18254" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="18340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18293" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18346" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18347" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="18352" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18353" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18353" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18354" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18356" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18356" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18357" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18359" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18361" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18367" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18368" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18372" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18373" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18378" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18379" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3031" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="18385" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18356" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18386" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="18390" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18391" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2886" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="18397" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18398" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6412" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="18419" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18353" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18420" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="18424" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18293" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18430" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18431" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="18437" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18437" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18438" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18440" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18442" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18447" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18452" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18437" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18453" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="18457" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18293" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18463" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18464" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3151" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="18468" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18469" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18469" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18470" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18472" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18472" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18473" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18475" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18475" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18479" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18479" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18482" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18484" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18493" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18494" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18498" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18499" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18504" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18475" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18507" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18510" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18526" class="Function">B≤lA</a>
  <a id="18517" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18526" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18526" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18531" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18533" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18472" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18535" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3836" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="18537" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18546" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18469" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18548" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18549" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18552" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18554" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18555" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="18560" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18526" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18565" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18567" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18568" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#8088" class="Function">lift-alg-≤-lift</a> <a id="18584" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18472" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18586" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18587" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18469" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18588" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="18591" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18479" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18597" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18293" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18604" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3229" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="18610" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18610" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18614" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18614" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18619" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18621" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5009" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18628" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18629" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18293" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18635" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18610" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18638" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18640" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18614" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="18646" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18293" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18652" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18653" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3292" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="18657" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18658" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18658" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18659" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18661" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18661" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18662" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18664" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18666" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18666" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="18669" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18671" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18673" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5314" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18679" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18680" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6463" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="18684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17570" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18690" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18664" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18691" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18694" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18707" class="Function">γ</a>
  <a id="18698" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="18707" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18707" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18709" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18711" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18720" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18658" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18723" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18728" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18729" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18731" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="18733" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18661" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
   <a id="18738" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18707" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18740" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18742" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4393" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="18750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18751" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18760" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18658" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18762" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18763" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18766" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18240" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18768" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18769" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18772" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18661" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18774" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18775" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2886" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="18781" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4857" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="18791" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18793" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18666" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19293" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="19300" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19300" class="Module">_</a> <a id="19302" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19305" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19307" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="19315" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19317" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19317" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19321" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19323" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="19324" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19326" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19326" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19330" href="Relations.Discrete.html#1408" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19335" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19336" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19344" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19346" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#525" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19347" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19349" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19352" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19353" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19356" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="19364" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19364" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19384" href="Algebras.Products.html#3936" class="Function">class-product</a><a id="19397" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19398" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19399" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19401" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19402" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19404" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19317" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19405" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19407" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19409" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19326" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19410" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19412" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19414" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="19415" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19416" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19419" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19420" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19422" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19426" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="19428" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19430" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19326" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19431" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="19435" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19364" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19453" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19455" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4083" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="19461" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19730" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19468" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19469" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6702" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="19472" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#544" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="19476" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19781" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="19481" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="19781" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19781" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19787" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19789" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19791" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19793" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19796" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19496" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19800" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19791" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19801" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19803" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1049" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="19805" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19806" href="Algebras.Products.html#3737" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19808" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19809" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19811" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19326" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19812" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19791" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19815" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19819" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19781" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="19825" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19825" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19827" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19829" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4393" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="19837" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19838" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19496" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19842" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19825" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19843" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19845" href="Algebras.Products.html#3737" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19847" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19848" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19850" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19326" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19851" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19853" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19825" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19854" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19856" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2886" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="19862" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4857" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19872" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19874" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2886" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="19880" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4857" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="19890" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

So, since `PS⊆SP`, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class `𝒦` belongs to `SP(𝒦)`.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="20023" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20023" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20041" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20043" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="20051" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20052" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="20055" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20056" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20058" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20059" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="20062" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20063" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20065" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20067" href="Algebras.Products.html#3936" class="Function">class-product</a><a id="20080" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20081" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20082" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20084" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19303" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20085" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20087" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19317" class="Bound">X</a><a id="20088" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="20090" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="20092" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19326" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20093" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20095" href="Relations.Discrete.html#2407" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="20097" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2940" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="20098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20099" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3629" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="20101" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19326" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20102" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="20105" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20023" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20123" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20123" class="Bound">fe</a> <a id="20126" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20128" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15827" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a><a id="20133" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20134" class="Argument">fe</a> <a id="20137" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20139" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#20123" class="Bound">fe</a><a id="20141" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20143" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19364" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>
